17 package org.http4s.ember.core.h2
18 
19 import cats._
20 import cats.effect._
21 import cats.effect.kernel.Outcome
22 import cats.syntax.all._
23 import fs2._
24 import fs2.io.net.Socket
25 import fs2.io.net.SocketException
26 import org.typelevel.log4cats.Logger
27 import scodec.bits._
28 
29 private[h2] class H2Connection[F[_]](
30     host: com.comcast.ip4s.Host,
31     port: com.comcast.ip4s.Port,
32     connectionType: H2Connection.ConnectionType,
33     localSettings: H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings,
34     val mapRef: Ref[F, Map[Int, H2Stream[F]]],
35     val state: Ref[F, H2Connection.State[F]], // odd if client, even if server
36     val outgoing: cats.effect.std.Queue[F, Chunk[H2Frame]],
37     // val outgoingData: cats.effect.std.Queue[F, Frame.Data], // TODO split data rather than backpressuring frames totally
38 
39     val createdStreams: cats.effect.std.Queue[F, Int],
40     val closedStreams: cats.effect.std.Queue[F, Int],
41     hpack: Hpack[F],
42     val streamCreateAndHeaders: Resource[F, Unit],
43     val settingsAck: Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings]],
44     acc: ByteVector, // Any Bytes Already Read
45     socket: Socket[F],
46     logger: Logger[F],
47 )(implicit F: Temporal[F]) {
48 
49   def initiateLocalStream: F[H2Stream[F]] = for {
50     t <- state.modify { s =>
51       val highestIsEven = s.highestStream % 2 == 0
52       val newHighest = connectionType match {
53         case H2Connection.ConnectionType.Server =>
54           if (highestIsEven) s.highestStream + 2 else s.highestStream + 1
55         case H2Connection.ConnectionType.Client =>
56           if (highestIsEven) s.highestStream + 1 else s.highestStream + 2
57       }
58       (s.copy(highestStream = newHighest), (s.remoteSettings, newHighest))
59     }
60     (settings, id) = t
61 
62     writeBlock <- Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, Unit]]
63     request <- Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, org.http4s.Request[fs2.Pure]]]
64     response <- Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, org.http4s.Response[fs2.Pure]]]
65     trailers <- Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, org.http4s.Headers]]
66     body <- cats.effect.std.Queue.unbounded[F, Either[Throwable, ByteVector]]
67     refState <- Ref.of[F, H2Stream.State[F]](
68       H2Stream.State(
69         H2Stream.StreamState.Idle,
70         settings.initialWindowSize.windowSize,
71         writeBlock,
72         localSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize,
73         request,
74         response,
75         trailers,
76         body,
77         None,
78       )
79     )
80     stream = new H2Stream(
81       id,
82       localSettings,
83       connectionType,
84       state.get.map(_.remoteSettings),
85       refState,
86       hpack,
87       outgoing,
88       closedStreams.offer(id),
89       goAway,
90       logger,
91     )
92     _ <- mapRef.update(m => m + (id -> stream))
93   } yield stream
94 
95   def initiateRemoteStreamById(id: Int): F[H2Stream[F]] = for {
96     t <- state.get.map(s => (s.remoteSettings, s.remoteHighestStream))
97     (settings, highestStream) = t
98     writeBlock <- Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, Unit]]
99     request <- Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, org.http4s.Request[fs2.Pure]]]
100     response <- Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, org.http4s.Response[fs2.Pure]]]
101     trailers <- Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, org.http4s.Headers]]
102     body <- cats.effect.std.Queue.unbounded[F, Either[Throwable, ByteVector]]
103     refState <- Ref.of[F, H2Stream.State[F]](
104       H2Stream.State(
105         H2Stream.StreamState.Idle,
106         settings.initialWindowSize.windowSize,
107         writeBlock,
108         localSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize,
109         request,
110         response,
111         trailers,
112         body,
113         None,
114       )
115     )
116     stream = new H2Stream(
117       id,
118       localSettings,
119       connectionType,
120       state.get.map(_.remoteSettings),
121       refState,
122       hpack,
123       outgoing,
124       closedStreams.offer(id),
125       goAway,
126       logger,
127     )
128     _ <- mapRef.update(m => m + (id -> stream))
129     _ <- state.update(s =>
130       s.copy(
131         highestStream = Math.max(s.highestStream, id),
132         remoteHighestStream = Math.max(s.remoteHighestStream, id),
133       )
134     )
135   } yield stream
136 
137   def goAway(error: H2Error): F[Unit] =
138     state.get.map(_.remoteHighestStream).flatMap { i =>
139       val g = error.toGoAway(i)
140       outgoing.offer(Chunk.singleton(g))
141     } >>
142       H2Connection.KillWithoutMessage().raiseError
143 
144   def writeLoop: Stream[F, Nothing] =
145     Stream
146       .fromQueueUnterminatedChunk[F, H2Frame](outgoing, Int.MaxValue)
147       .chunks
148       .evalMap { chunk =>
149         def go(chunk: Chunk[H2Frame]): F[Unit] = state.get.flatMap { s =>
150           val fullDataSize = chunk.foldLeft(0) {
151             case (init, H2Frame.Data(_, data, _, _)) => init + data.size.toInt
152             case (init, _) => init
153           }
154           // println(s"Next Write Block Window - data: $fullDataSize window:${s.writeWindow} $s")
155 
156           if (fullDataSize <= s.writeWindow && s.writeWindow > 0) {
157             val bv = chunk.foldLeft(ByteVector.empty) { case (acc, frame) =>
158               acc ++ H2Frame.toByteVector(frame)
159             }
160             state.update(s => s.copy(writeWindow = s.writeWindow - fullDataSize)) >>
161               socket.isOpen.ifM(
162                 socket.write(Chunk.byteVector(bv)) >>
163                   chunk.traverse_(frame => logger.debug(s"$host:$port Write - $frame")),
164                 new SocketException("Socket closed when attempting to write").raiseError,
165               )
166           } else {
167             val (nonData, after) = chunk.indexWhere(_.isInstanceOf[H2Frame.Data]) match {
168               case None => (chunk, Chunk.empty[H2Frame])
169               case Some(ix) => chunk.splitAt(ix)
170             }
171 
172             val bv = nonData.foldLeft(ByteVector.empty) { case (acc, frame) =>
173               acc ++ H2Frame.toByteVector(frame)
174             }
175             socket.isOpen.ifM(
176               socket.write(Chunk.byteVector(bv)) >>
177                 nonData.traverse_(frame => logger.debug(s"$host:$port Write - $frame")),
178               new SocketException("Socket closed when attempting to write").raiseError,
179             ) >>
180               s.writeBlock.get.rethrow >>
181               go(after)
182           }
183         }
184         val firstGoAway = chunk.collectFirst { case g: H2Frame.GoAway =>
185           mapRef.get.flatMap { m =>
186             m.values.toList.traverse_(connection => connection.receiveGoAway(g))
187           } >> state.update(s => s.copy(closed = true))
188         }
189         firstGoAway.getOrElse(F.unit) >> go(chunk)
190       }
191       .drain
192   // TODO Split Frames between Data and Others Hold Data If we are at cap
193   //  Currently will backpressure at the data frame till its cleared
194 
195   def readLoop: F[Unit] = {
196     def connectionTerminated: String = s"Connection $host:$port readLoop Terminated"
197     val readFromSocket: F[Option[Chunk[Byte]]] =
198       socket.read(localSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize)
199 
200     def readNextFrame(acc: ByteVector): F[Option[(H2Frame, ByteVector)]] =
201       if (acc.isEmpty) {
202         readFromSocket.flatMap {
203           case Some(chunk) => readNextFrame(chunk.toByteVector)
204           case None =>
205             logger.debug(s"$connectionTerminated with empty").as(None)
206         }
207       } else
208         H2Frame.RawFrame.fromByteVector(acc) match {
209           case Some((raw, leftover)) =>
210             H2Frame.fromRaw(raw) match {
211               case Right(frame) => F.pure(Some((frame, leftover)))
212               case Left(e) =>
213                 logger.warn(s"$connectionTerminated invalid Raw to Frame $e") >>
214                   goAway(e) >> F.pure(None)
215             }
216           case None =>
217             readFromSocket.flatMap {
218               case Some(chunk) => readNextFrame(acc ++ chunk.toByteVector)
219               case None => logger.debug(s"$connectionTerminated with $acc").as(None)
220             }
221         }
222 
223     def processFrame(frame: H2Frame, s: H2Connection.State[F]): F[Unit] = (frame, s) match {
224       // Headers and Continuation Frames are Stateful
225       // Headers if not closed MUST
226       case (
227             c @ H2Frame.Continuation(id, true, _),
228             H2Connection.State(_, _, _, _, _, _, _, Some((h, cs)), None),
229           ) =>
230         if (h.identifier == id) {
231           state.update(s => s.copy(headersInProgress = None)) >>
232             mapRef.get.map(_.get(id)).flatMap {
233               case Some(s) =>
234                 s.receiveHeaders(h, cs ::: c :: Nil: _*)
235               case None =>
236                 streamCreateAndHeaders.use(_ =>
237                   for {
238                     stream <- initiateRemoteStreamById(id)
239                     _ <- createdStreams.offer(id)
240                     _ <- stream.receiveHeaders(h, cs ::: c :: Nil: _*)
241                   } yield ()
242                 )
243             }
244         } else {
245           logger.warn("Invalid Continuation - Protocol Error - Issuing GoAway") >>
246             goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
247         }
248       case (
249             c @ H2Frame.Continuation(id, true, _),
250             H2Connection.State(_, _, _, _, _, _, _, None, Some((p, cs))),
251           ) =>
252         if (p.promisedStreamId == id) {
253           state.update(s => s.copy(headersInProgress = None)) >>
254             mapRef.get.map(_.get(id)).flatMap {
255               case Some(s) =>
256                 s.receivePushPromise(p, cs ::: c :: Nil: _*)
257               case None =>
258                 streamCreateAndHeaders.use(_ =>
259                   for {
260                     stream <- initiateRemoteStreamById(id)
261                     _ <- createdStreams.offer(id)
262                     _ <- stream.receivePushPromise(p, cs ::: c :: Nil: _*)
263 
264                   } yield ()
265                 )
266             }
267         } else {
268           logger.warn("Invalid Continuation - Protocol Error - Issuing GoAway") >>
269             goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
270         }
271       case (
272             c @ H2Frame.Continuation(id, false, _),
273             H2Connection.State(_, _, _, _, _, _, _, None, Some((h, cs))),
274           ) =>
275         if (h.identifier == id) {
276           state.update(s => s.copy(pushPromiseInProgress = (h, cs ::: c :: Nil).some))
277         } else {
278           logger.warn("Invalid Continuation - Protocol Error - Issuing GoAway") >>
279             goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
280         }
281 
282       case (
283             c @ H2Frame.Continuation(id, false, _),
284             H2Connection.State(_, _, _, _, _, _, _, Some((h, cs)), None),
285           ) =>
286         if (h.identifier == id) {
287           state.update(s => s.copy(headersInProgress = (h, cs ::: c :: Nil).some))
288         } else {
289           logger.warn("Invalid Continuation - Protocol Error - Issuing GoAway") >>
290             goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
291         }
292       case (f, H2Connection.State(_, _, _, _, _, _, _, Some(_), None)) =>
293         // Only Continuation Frames Are Valid While there is a value
294         logger.warn(
295           s"Continuation for headers in process, retrieved unexpected frame $f -  Protocol Error - Issuing GoAway"
296         ) >>
297           goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
298       case (f, H2Connection.State(_, _, _, _, _, _, _, None, Some(_))) =>
299         // Only Continuation Frames Are Valid While there is a value
300         logger.warn(
301           s"Continuation for push promise in process, retrieved unexpected frame $f -  Protocol Error - Issuing GoAway"
302         ) >>
303           goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
304 
305       case (h @ H2Frame.Headers(i, sd, _, true, headerBlock, _), s) =>
306         val size = headerBlock.size.toInt
307         if (size > s.remoteSettings.maxFrameSize.frameSize) {
308           logger.warn("Header Size too large for frame size - FrameSizeError - Issuing GoAway") >>
309             goAway(H2Error.FrameSizeError)
310         } else if (sd.exists(s => s.dependency == i)) {
311           goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
312         } else {
313           mapRef.get.map(_.get(i)).flatMap {
314             case Some(s) =>
315               s.receiveHeaders(h)
316             case None =>
317               val isValidToCreate = connectionType match {
318                 case H2Connection.ConnectionType.Server => i % 2 != 0
319                 case H2Connection.ConnectionType.Client => i % 2 == 0
320               }
321               if (!isValidToCreate || i <= s.remoteHighestStream) {
322                 logger.warn(
323                   s"Not Valid Stream to Create $i - $isValidToCreate, ${s.highestStream} - Protocol Error - Issuing GoAway"
324                 ) >>
325                   goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
326               } else {
327                 streamCreateAndHeaders.use(_ =>
328                   for {
329                     stream <- initiateRemoteStreamById(i)
330                     _ <- createdStreams.offer(i)
331                     _ <- stream.receiveHeaders(h)
332 
333                   } yield ()
334                 )
335               }
336           }
337         }
338       case (h @ H2Frame.Headers(i, sd, _, false, headerBlock, _), s) =>
339         val size = headerBlock.size.toInt
340         if (size > s.remoteSettings.maxFrameSize.frameSize) goAway(H2Error.FrameSizeError)
341         else if (sd.exists(s => s.dependency == i)) goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
342         else {
343           state.update(s => s.copy(headersInProgress = Some((h, List.empty))))
344         }
345       case (h @ H2Frame.PushPromise(_, true, i, headerBlock, _), s) =>
346         val size = headerBlock.size.toInt
347         if (connectionType == H2Connection.ConnectionType.Server) {
348           logger.warn(
349             "Encountered Push Promise Frame a a Server - Protocol Error - Issuing GoAway"
350           ) >>
351             goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
352         } else if (size > s.remoteSettings.maxFrameSize.frameSize) {
353           logger.warn("Header Size too large for frame size - FrameSizeError - Issuing GoAway") >>
354             goAway(H2Error.FrameSizeError)
355         } else {
356           mapRef.get.map(_.get(i)).flatMap {
357             case Some(s) =>
358               s.receivePushPromise(h)
359             case None =>
360               val isValidToCreate = i % 2 == 0
361               if (!isValidToCreate || i <= s.remoteHighestStream) {
362                 logger.warn(
363                   s"Not Valid Stream to Create $i - $isValidToCreate, ${s.remoteHighestStream} - Protocol Error - Issuing GoAway"
364                 )
365                 goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
366               } else {
367                 streamCreateAndHeaders.use(_ =>
368                   for {
369                     stream <- initiateRemoteStreamById(i)
370                     _ <- createdStreams.offer(i)
371                     _ <- stream.receivePushPromise(h)
372                   } yield ()
373                 )
374               }
375           }
376         }
377       case (h @ H2Frame.PushPromise(_, false, _, headerBlock, _), s) =>
378         val size = headerBlock.size.toInt
379         if (size > s.remoteSettings.maxFrameSize.frameSize) goAway(H2Error.FrameSizeError)
380         else {
381           state.update(s => s.copy(pushPromiseInProgress = Some((h, List.empty))))
382         }
383 
384       case (H2Frame.Continuation(_, _, _), _) =>
385         goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
386 
387       case (settings @ H2Frame.Settings(0, false, _), _) =>
388         for {
389           newWriteBlock <- Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, Unit]]
390           t <- state.modify { s =>
391             val newSettings = H2Frame.Settings.updateSettings(settings, s.remoteSettings)
392             val differenceInWindow =
393               newSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize - s.remoteSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize
394             (
395               s.copy(
396                 remoteSettings = newSettings,
397                 writeWindow = s.writeWindow,
398                 writeBlock = newWriteBlock,
399               ),
400               (newSettings, differenceInWindow, s.writeBlock),
401             )
402           }
403           (settings, difference, oldWriteBlock) = t
404           _ <- oldWriteBlock.complete(Either.right(()))
405           _ <- mapRef.get.flatMap { map =>
406             map.toList.traverse { case (_, stream) =>
407               stream.modifyWriteWindow(difference)
408             }
409           }
410           _ <- outgoing.offer(Chunk.singleton(H2Frame.Settings.Ack))
411           _ <- settingsAck.complete(Either.right(settings)).void
412 
413         } yield ()
414       case (H2Frame.Settings(0, true, _), _) => Applicative[F].unit
415       case (H2Frame.Settings(_, _, _), _) =>
416         logger.warn("Received Settings Not Oriented at Identifier 0 - Issuing goAway") >>
417           goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
418       case (g @ H2Frame.GoAway(0, _, _, _), _) =>
419         mapRef.get.flatMap { m =>
420           m.values.toList.traverse_(connection => connection.receiveGoAway(g))
421         } >> outgoing.offer(Chunk.singleton(H2Frame.Ping.ack))
422       case (_: H2Frame.GoAway, _) =>
423         goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
424       case (H2Frame.Ping(0, false, bv), _) =>
425         outgoing.offer(Chunk.singleton(H2Frame.Ping.ack.copy(data = bv)))
426       case (H2Frame.Ping(0, true, _), _) => Applicative[F].unit
427       case (H2Frame.Ping(_, _, _), _) =>
428         goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
429 
430       case (H2Frame.WindowUpdate(_, 0), _) =>
431         logger.warn("Encountered 0 Sized Window Update - Procol Error - Issuing GoAway") >>
432           goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
433       case (w @ H2Frame.WindowUpdate(i, size), _) =>
434         i match {
435           case 0 =>
436             for {
437               newWriteBlock <- Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, Unit]]
438               t <- state.modify { s =>
439                 val newSize = s.writeWindow + size
440                 val sizeValid =
441                   (s.writeWindow >= 0 && newSize >= 0) || s.writeWindow < 0 // Less than 2^31-1 and didn't overflow, going negative
442                 (
443                   s.copy(writeBlock = newWriteBlock, writeWindow = s.writeWindow + size),
444                   (s.writeBlock, sizeValid),
445                 )
446               }
447               (oldWriteBlock, valid) = t
448               _ <- oldWriteBlock.complete(Right(()))
449               _ <- {
450                 if (!valid) goAway(H2Error.FlowControlError)
451                 else outgoing.offer(Chunk.singleton(H2Frame.Ping.ack))
452               }
453             } yield ()
454           case otherwise =>
455             mapRef.get.map(_.get(otherwise)).flatMap {
456               case Some(s) =>
457                 s.receiveWindowUpdate(w)
458               case None =>
459                 logger.warn(s"Received WindowUpdate for Closed or Idle Stream - $w, $i") >>
460                   goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
461             }
462         }
463 
464       case (d @ H2Frame.Data(i, data, _, _), _) =>
465         val size = data.size.toInt
466         if (size > localSettings.maxFrameSize.frameSize) {
467           logger.warn(
468             "Receive Data Size Larger than Allowed Frame Size - Frame Size Error - Issuing GoAway"
469           ) >>
470             goAway(H2Error.FrameSizeError)
471         } else {
472           mapRef.get.map(_.get(i)).flatMap {
473             case Some(s) =>
474               for {
475                 st <- state.get
476                 newSize = st.readWindow - d.data.size.toInt
477 
478                 needsWindowUpdate = newSize <= (localSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize / 2)
479                 _ <- state.update(s =>
480                   s.copy(readWindow =
481                     if (needsWindowUpdate) localSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize
482                     else newSize.toInt
483                   )
484                 )
485                 _ <-
486                   if (needsWindowUpdate)
487                     outgoing.offer(
488                       Chunk.singleton(
489                         H2Frame.WindowUpdate(
490                           0,
491                           st.remoteSettings.initialWindowSize.windowSize - newSize.toInt,
492                         )
493                       )
494                     )
495                   else Applicative[F].unit
496                 _ <- s.receiveData(d)
497               } yield ()
498             case None =>
499               logger.warn(
500                 s"Received Data Frame for Idle or Closed Stream $i - Protocol Error - Issuing GoAway"
501               ) >>
502                 goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
503           }
504         }
505 
506       case (rst @ H2Frame.RstStream(i, _), _) =>
507         mapRef.get.map(_.get(i)).flatMap {
508           case Some(s) =>
509             s.receiveRstStream(rst)
510           case None =>
511             logger.warn(
512               s"Received RstStream for Idle or Closed Stream $i - Protocol Error - Issuing GoAway"
513             ) >>
514               goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError)
515         }
516       case (H2Frame.Priority(i, _, i2, _), _) =>
517         if (i == i2) goAway(H2Error.ProtocolError) // Can't depend on yourself
518         else Applicative[F].unit // We Do Nothing with these presently
519       case (H2Frame.Unknown(_), _) => Applicative[F].unit // Ignore Unknown Frames
520     }
521 
522     def readLoopAux(acc: ByteVector): F[Unit] =
523       readNextFrame(acc).flatMap {
524         case Some((frame, nacc)) =>
525           logger.debug(s"$host:$port Read - $frame") >>
526             state.get.flatMap(processFrame(frame, _)) >>
527             readLoopAux(nacc)
528         case None => F.unit
529       }
530 
531     F.guaranteeCase(readLoopAux(acc)) {
532       case Outcome.Errored(H2Connection.KillWithoutMessage()) =>
533         logger.debug(s"ReadLoop has received that is should kill") >>
534           state.update(s => s.copy(closed = true))
535       case Outcome.Errored(e) =>
536         logger.error(e)(s"ReadLoop has errored") >>
537           goAway(H2Error.InternalError) >>
538           state.update(s => s.copy(closed = true))
539 
540       case _ => state.update(s => s.copy(closed = true))
541     }
542   }
543 
544 }
545 
546 private[h2] object H2Connection {
547   final case class State[F[_]](
548       remoteSettings: H2Frame.Settings.ConnectionSettings,
549       writeWindow: Int,
550       writeBlock: Deferred[F, Either[Throwable, Unit]],
551       readWindow: Int,
552       highestStream: Int,
553       remoteHighestStream: Int,
554       closed: Boolean,
555       headersInProgress: Option[(H2Frame.Headers, List[H2Frame.Continuation])],
556       pushPromiseInProgress: Option[(H2Frame.PushPromise, List[H2Frame.Continuation])],
557   )
558 
559   final case class KillWithoutMessage()
560       extends RuntimeException
561       with scala.util.control.NoStackTrace
562 
563   sealed trait ConnectionType
564   object ConnectionType {
565     case object Server extends ConnectionType
566     case object Client extends ConnectionType
567   }
568 
569 }
